## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="6abea-1610">Commenti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6abea-1610">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6abea-1611">La classe **MS-DFSR-member** fa parte del supporto del servizio di replica file System distribuito (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6abea-1611">The **ms-DFSR-Member** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
